 darasal, vah itnaa aasaan he nahin jaisaa dekhte hai
 The process of taking a sample in an exit poll or survey is quite cumbersome
 sampling ko samajhane se pehle ham agsit pole, post pole survey or opinian pole ko jaananaa chahie
 What are exit polls? Exit poll results are always released on the last day of voting
 haalanki data collection jis din voting hoti he us din bhi kiya jaataa he
 On the day of voting of the last face, when the voter is leaving for the vote, he is asked who he voted for
 is aadhaar par kiye gaye surveykshan se jo vyapak nattejey nikaale jate hai
 This is called exit poll
 aamtaur par tivi channel voting ke aakhri din agsit pole hi dikhaate hai
 What are Post Polls? Post poll exit results are more accurate
 agsit pole main survey agency matdaan ke turant baad matadaata se raay jaanakar motaa-motaa hisaab laga leti hai
 Whereas post polls are always the next day or one or two days after the voting
 jaise maan lijie 6wein charan kii voting 12 may ko hui thi
 If the survey agency tries to get their opinion from the voters who voted in this phase by May 13, 14, or 15, then it is called post poll
 post pole kyon hote hai zyada sateek?agsit pole main matadaataaon ke vot dene ke turant baad unki raay jaanane kii koshish kii jaati he
 The survey people do this survey only outside the polling booth
 isliye matadaata apni pahchaan chhupate hue hadabadi main raay bataa dete hai joki jaruri nahin ki sahi hi ho
 Whereas in the post poll, a day later, after talking to the voter, he tries to find his mind, to which candidate he has voted
 is dauraan vah kisi kanfusion main nahin hota he or lagbhag sahi-sahi raay bataa detaa he
 Opinion polopinian poles are different from exit pols
 opinian pole kaa sabase zyada istemaal patrkaar, chunavi survey karne vaali agenciyaan karti hai
 Through this, journalists used to find the pulse of the public in various issues, issues and elections
 shrey jorge galop or claude robinson sabase pehle iskaa istemaal kiya tha
 Know how is sampling for a poll? Field work is the biggest task in preparing an opion poll
 isaki sampling ke liye chunavi survey karne vaali agency karmchaaree aam logon se milte hai or kuch sawaal poochhate hai
 Candidate is good or bad
 is aadhaar par bhi ek motaa-moti raay jaan lee jaati he
 At the same time, people who are involved in this process are also given a form to fill
 form ko bharwane kii bhi ek lambii prakriya hoti he
 The identity of the voters remains secret and they feel free to give their opinion
 aise main unke liye silband dibba rakhaa jaataa he
 So that they put a full form about the candidate of their choice
 opinian pole main sabase mahatvapurn cheez sampling hoti he
 Sampling means the opinions from which people have been or will be tried
 loksabhaa chunaav 2019: jaaniye kya hote hai agsit pole, kaise nikalate hai aankadekaise hoti he sampling, kya he prakriya?opinian pole main sirf kuch logon kii raay par nattejey nahin nikaale ja sakate hai
 Methodology will be different for different states, legislatures and region-specific sampling
 jaise madhyapradesh, uttar pradesh or bihar main sampling kaa aadhaar alag-alag hoga
 Because in UP and Bihar, the person who will be trying to know his opinion will also have to take care of the social background, caste and religion of that person
 agar soshal becoground, cast or relijan ko dhyaan main rakhkar survey kiya jaae to 5000 ke sample sies se bhi sateek nishkarsh par pahunchaa ja saktaa he
 Whereas in Madhya Pradesh, the sampling of caste voters will be other than this
 vahiin upi-bihar main muslim or dalit bahulya aabaadi vaale kshetron main unki aabaadi ke pratishat ke hisaab se random sample liya jayega
 What is random sampling? Large survey agencies of the country resort to random sampling
 isamen seat, booth str par or matadaata str par random sampling hoti he
 Suppose there are 2000 voters at a booth
 usamen se 100 logon kaa intervyuu karnaa he
 So these 100 people will be included in a random way
 iske liye do hajaar kaa 100 se bhaag diya to 20 bachaa
 After this, one of the voters list will take such a number on a random basis, which is less than 20
 jaise maan lijie aapane 12 liya
 So the voter who will be at number 12 in the voter list will be the first sampling candidate whose interview agency will interview
 phir us sankhya 12 main 20, 20 ,20 jodate jate hai or matadaata kaa intervyuu kiya jaataa he
 This is random sampling
 kin-kin madhyamon se hoti he sampling?opinian pole jaanane ke liye field ke saath hi akhabaaron main bhi ek form diya jaataa tha
 Which was filled and sent to the address
 vakt badalane ke saath hi technology badalati gai or sampling kaa tarika bhi thodaa-thodaa badalte gaya
 Many survey agencies are now sampling phone calls, SMS online as well
 haalanki, bharat ke sandarbh main phone kol sampling behad kargar nahin kyonki iske jariye sahi jaankaree mili yah jaruri nahin
 That's why sampling based on interviews gives more or less accurate results

 group discshan main kya karen or kya nahin1
 Keep the contact while speaking; In addition to making only the contact from the moderator while speaking, keep the contact from all the people present in the discussion
 2
 Start GD It has often been seen that it is often beneficial to start in group discussion

 3
 Speak clearly: Sometimes people want to speak a lot, but because of not being able to speak clearly, the whole matter goes awry

 4
 discshan ko trek par laane kii koshish carendiscshan main aisa kai baar hota he ki sari bahes vishay se vishyantar ho jaataa he

 5
 Maintain Positive Attitude Maintain Confidence
 kisi par bina vajah chadhane kii koshish na karen

 6
 Speak intelligently so that during your speaking, it is as if you are speaking only to cut your share time

 7
 dusron ko bhi sammaan se sunengroup discshan main logon ko sunne se bhi kai baar kai link mil jate hai jo aapako aage or behatar tareeke se bolne ke points de detaa he
 In such a situation, you create a special space for yourself
 8
 Do not go into too much detail, it happens many times that we are getting to know a lot on many topics and the debate on that topic starts as soon as it starts
 na dusron kii sunate hai or na hi unhen bolne kaa mauka dete hai
 Avoid monologues in group discussion
 9
 Wear formal clothesinterview and group discussion is not a fancy dress competition, so be careful
 10
 Maintain sobriety Maintaining sobriety is very important from the beginning of the group discussion to the end

 party adhyaksh sonia gandhi ne pichley saptaah congress ke anusuchit jati vibhaag ke varisht padaadhikariyon ke saath mulaakaat kii thi jisamen unhen daliton ke bich party ke aadhaar ko majboot banane ke liye teji se kaam karne kaa nirdesh diya gaya tha
 According to Nitin Raut, the head of the Congress's Scheduled Castes department, Sonia Gandhi said that her organization is going to work on many levels to mobilize the Dalit society, including appointing a coordinator in every assembly constituency and taking out the 'swabhiman Yatra' from the constitution
 is
 raut ne ''pitiai-bhashaa'' ko bataaya, ''ham sitambar ke pehle saptaah tak maharashtra, jharkhand or haryana main apane vibhaag ke samanvayakon kii niyukti kar denge
